| Embrace of the Serpent<br/><br/>It almost feels like a religious experience, watching a movie that's as beautifully alien and removed from convention as Embrace of the Serpent. Colombian filmmaker Ciro Guerra's Amazon-set drama is an indignant lament on the devastating, festering effects of colonialism, but it's more experiential and less studious than that sounds. The black-and-white river imagery is supple, hypnotic and frightening, in that startling way that most unfamiliar things are, at first, frightening. The scariest thing, though, is how vividly Guerra shows us—via two white men's parallel river quests, separated by 40 years—the extent of the destruction pale-skinned conquerors wreaked on the indigenous cultures of the region. Even scarier: the realization that the eradication of our indigenous people, in our America, makes Guerra's dark fable hit uncomfortably close to home.<br/><br/>Like the narrative (which is based on a pair of white explorer's real-life journals), the production's heroes are dual, with cinematographer David Gallego having as much influence on the film's success as Guerra. With locations as lush as the ones we glide and trudge through on the winding South American riverways, it seems best, for a story this restrained and contemplative, for us to simply, respectfully bear witness to the indescribably beautiful surroundings. There's no need to breathe life into what's already teeming with overly stylized presentation, and thankfully, Gallego's got taste. The choice to go monochrome supports the thrust of the story; what would have been about color and vibrancy is now all about light, darkness and shadow.<br/><br/>At the center of the first story is Theodor Koch-Grunberg (Jan Bijvoet), a German explorer in search of a rare, sacred flower called the "yakuna." Theo's fallen ill on his expedition, tended to by his local guide, Manduca (Miguel Dionisio Ramos). As they land their boat onto the riverbank, they're met by Karamakate (Nilbio Torres), a shaman who doesn't take kindly to white men, whose violent conquest has rendered him a companionless river dweller, the last of his tribe. Locals like Manduca, who cooperate with the whites and have adopted many of their Western customs are, to him, just as disgusting. Reluctantly, Karamakate agrees to be their guide (only he knows how to reach the yakuna), enticed by Theo's promise to help him find the last remaining survivors of his tribe, who the German claims he's seen with his own eyes.<br/><br/>On their journey, the cultural divide is slowly bridged: Karamakate keeps Theo's illness at bay with herbal medicine; Theo shares some of the worldly belongings he's hauling around in his clunky luggage box. (Meanwhile, Manduca straddles the cultural line.) Their bond is shaken to the core when they come across a grove of drained rubber trees and indigenous workers mutilated and enslaved by the invaders. Tensions are heightened again when they happen upon a Catholic mission where a mad Spanish priest rules over orphaned indigenous children, forcing them to abandon their old customs as he abuses them on a whim in a multitude of sickening ways. This portion of the film is almost unbearably awful to watch. It speaks to Guerra's integrity, though, that he shows no measure of restraint in depicting something so horrible as cultural extermination. Again, the true horror is how easily linked the priest's child abuse is to issues of our time (Spotlight comes to mind).<br/><br/>Theo has a mental breakdown when his compass is stolen by one of the locals, fearing the technological trinket will sully the purity of the tribes traditions. Karamakate takes the fit as a sign of ignorant condescension, and they're back to square one. Our link to the second story, set in the 1940s, is Karamakate, the older version of whom is played by Antonio Bolivar. We flash over to this second journey intermittently, which sees the shaman in a sorry state of soullessness, numbed to nothing by the continuing white-man takeover. He meets a new, American explorer, Evans (Brionne Davis), who, like Theo, is trekking towards the yakuna wonder-plant. The tone's much more pensive and dirge-like in this less-eventful second story, which is mostly about the sorrow that's built up in Karamakate following decades of watching his home ravaged by Western "progress."<br/><br/>As grim and yucky as this all sounds, the movie isn't without a few moments of mirth. Evans blowing Karamakate's goddamn mind with a phonograph under a starry night sky is heart-meltingly cute, and when young Karamakate and Theo exchange the occasional glance of recognition and acceptance at each other, it gives the story just the right amount of hopefulness it needs to avoid being completely depressing. What'll be most challenging about the film for many is its pace, which is relatively lax and often stretches moments and shots longer than normal. Some would call this meandering; I'd call it glamorously introspective (I have no qualms about staring at Gallego's images for an extra beat or two—or three). Guerra's made a magical film in that it feels strangely organic and of the earth. The mechanisms we're used to recognizing and latching on to—performances, camera moves, editing, sound design—flow together so naturally in Guerra and his team's hands that Embrace of the Serpent feels of the earth, not of 35mm celluloid. | Glacadh leis an nathair<br/><br/>Mothaíonn sé beagnach cosúil le eispéireas reiligiúnach, ag breathnú ar scannán atá chomh eachtrannach álainn agus a bhaint as an gcompord mar Glacadh leis an Sáirsint. Is é an scannánóir Colóime Ciro Guerra's Amazon-a leagtar dráma le haghaidh maisithe le locht, éifeachtaí cloéinseacha á bhrath, ach tá sé níos mó turgnamhach agus níos lú stiúideo ná sin fuaimeanna. Tá na híomhánna abhann dubh-agus-bán forlíonta, hypnotic agus scanrúil, ar an mbealach tosaigh sin go bhfuil na rudaí is suntasaí, ar dtús, scanrúil. Is é an rud is géire, áfach, cé chomh beoga Guerra a thaispeánann dúinn - trí dhá quests abhann comhthreomhara fir, arna scaradh ag 40 bliain - méid na gcoiteoirí scriosta pale-craic a ndearnadh neamhaird orthu ar chultúir dhúchasacha an réigiúin. Fiú níos géire: an réadú go mbuaileann ár ndaoine dúchasacha, inár Meiriceá, go bhfuil an t-imeacht dorcha Gera ar siúl go míchompordach sa bhaile.<br/><br/>Cosúil leis an scéal (atá bunaithe ar péire irisí fíor-saoil an taiscéalaí bán), tá laochra an léiriúcháin déach, le ceamaradóir David Galego a bhfuil an oiread tionchair aige ar rath an scannáin mar Ghúera. Le suíomhanna mar lush mar na cinn a spícímid agus a bhí ag dul tríd ar bhealaí aibhneacha Mheiriceá Theas a fhoirceannadh, is cosúil is fearr, le haghaidh scéal a chuir srian air seo agus níos iomaíche, go simplí dúinn, finné a iompróidh go measúil ar an timpeallacht neamh-inscríofa álainn. Níl aon ghá leis an saol a análú ina bhfuil an cur i láthair ró-shealbhaithe cheana féin, agus le buíochas, blas a fuair Galego. Tacaíonn an rogha dul monacrómach le sá an scéil; is é an rud a bheadh faoi dhath agus beogacht anois ar fad faoi sholas, dorchadas agus scáth.<br/><br/>Ag croílár an chéad scéal tá Theodore Koch-Grunberg (Jan Bijvote), taiscéalaí Gearmánach sa tóir ar annamh, bláthanna naofa ar a dtugtar an "yakuna." Thin fill Theo ar a thuras, dírithe ar a threoir áitiúil, Manda (Miguel Dionio Ramos). Agus iad ag teacht amach ar bhád chuig an bhruach abhann, bhuail Kamakate (Nilbio Torres), chun na ndaoine sin nach dtógann go cineálta le fir bhána, a ndearna dweller abhann gan chompánach dó, an ceann deireanach dá threibh. Is iad muintir na háite cosúil le Manda, a théann i gcomhar leis na whites agus a bhfuil go leor dá gcuid custaim an Iarthair glactha acu, leis, chomh disgusting. Go drogall orthu, aontaíonn Karamakate gur treoir dóibh (ach níl a fhios aige conas a bhaint amach an yakuna), faoi i ndáiríre geallaimid cabhrú leis teacht ar an marthanóirí deireanach a threibh, a mhaíonn na Gearmáine go bhfaca sé lena shúile féin.<br/><br/>Ar a dturas, tá an roinnte cultúrtha droichead mall: Coinníonn Karamakate tinneas Theo ar bhá le leigheas luibhe; Roinneann Theo roinnt de na giuirléidí domhanda atá á n-úsáid aige ina bhosca bagáiste cluky (Idir an dá linn, cuireann Manda an líne chultúrtha i bhfeidhm.) Tá a nasc briste go dtí an croí nuair a thagann siad trasna ar an groove de chrainn rubair draenáilte agus oibrithe dúchasacha mutated agus enslaveed ag an ionróirí. Tarlaíonn sé arís nuair a tharlaíonn siad ar mhisean Caitliceach nuair a rialaíonn sagart mór na Spáinne níos mó ná leanaí dúchasacha a dílleachtaí, ag cur orthu a gcuid custaim d'aois mar mí-úsáid sé iad ar whim ar an iliomad bealaí tosting. Tá an chuid seo den scannán beagnach uafásach uafásach le féachaint ar.B labhraíonn sé le hionracas Gúerra, áfach, nach léiríonn sé aon bheart srianta i rud éigin chomh uafásach a thaispeáint mar rud éigin chéasadh. Arís, is é an fíor-uafás cé chomh héasca agus atá baint mí-úsáid an sagart ar cheisteanna ar ár gcuid ama (taibhsítear Spotlight le hintinn).<br/><br/>Tá briseadh intinne ag Theo nuair a ghoideann duine de mhuintir na háite a chompáis, agus ag eagla go dtiocfaidh íonacht na dtreibheanna ar an traein. Is é an nasc atá againn leis an dara scéal atá againn, atá leagtha síos sna 1940idí, ná Karamakate, an leagan is sine díobh a imríonn Antonio Bolivar. Táimid ag flash ar láimh go dtí an dara turas ar feadh tréimhse éiginnte, a fheiceann an shaman i staid brón an soulless, nainmnigh aon rud ag an leanúnach bán-fear ghlacadóir. Buaileann sé le taiscéalaí nua Meiriceánach, Evans (Brinne Davis), atá, cosúil le Theo, ag fálróid i dtreo an ghléasra iontas yakuna. An ton ar i bhfad níos mó bríomhar agus fearg-mhaith sa dara scéal seo níos lú-tráthúil, a bhfuil den chuid is mó mar gheall ar an brón go tógtha i Karamate tar éis fiche nó tríocha bliain de faire ar a bhaile ravaged ag an Iarthair "dul chun cinn."<br/><br/>Mar grim agus ky mar seo go léir fuaimeanna, nach bhfuil an scannán gan cúpla nóiméad de a bhráithre. Tá sé gleoite ar intinn ag Evans ag séideadh ar dhiadamkate Karamakate le grianghraf faoi spéir oíche réalta, agus nuair a dhéanann tú Karamatate agus Theo mhalartú ar an amharc ó am go chéile, tugann sé an scéal ach an méid ceart dóchasacha a chaithfidh sé a sheachaint a bheith go hiomlán brónach. Is é an rud is dúshlánaí faoin scannán do go leor ná a luas, atá réasúnta suaimhneach agus a chuireann deireadh le chuimhneacháin agus shots níos faide ná mar is gnách. Bheadh roinnt glaoch ar an meirciú seo; ba mhaith liom glaoch air go glamorous neamh-inghníomhach (níl aon chéibh agam faoi starring ag íomhánna Gallego le haghaidh buille breise nó dhó-nó trí cinn).Déantar le scannán draíochta go mbraitheann sé go aisteach orgánach agus an domhain. Na meicníochtaí a úsáidtear muid a aithint agus a suímh ar a — léirithe, bogann ceamara, eagarthóireacht, dearadh fuaime - sreabhadh le chéile chomh nádúrtha i Gera agus a fhoireann ar láimh go Measann an Seilide an domhain, ní de 35mm cellooid. |
| Regensburgis a city in south-east Germany, situated at the confluence of the Danube, Naab and Regen rivers. With over 140,000 inhabitants, Regensburg is the fourth-largest city in the State of Bavaria (from Latin Castra Regina, also lat. Ratisbona and RatisponaThe city has a population of 150,894 (December 31, 2017) and is thus fourth after Munich, Nuremberg and Augsburg . The city is the political, economic and cultural centre of Eastern Bavaria and the capital of the Bavarian administrative region Upper Palatinate. The medieval centre of the city is a UNESCO World Heritage Site and a testimony of the city's status as cultural centre of southern Germany in the Middle Ages. In 2014, Regensburg was among the top sights and travel attractions in Germany.[1] Generally known in English as Ratisbon until well into the twentieth century, the city is known as Ratisbonne in French and as Ratisbona in Italian, Portuguese and Spanish. among the large cities of the Free State of Bavaria.<br/><br/>It is the episcopal see of the diocese Regensburg, has three universities and is one of the 3 regional centers in Bavaria. [1]<br/><br/>The climate in Regensburg is categorized in the Köppen climate classification as Dfb (humid continental). The average temperature of 8.5 °C is slightly above the German average (7.8 °C), the average precipitation of 636 mm per year below the German average (approximately 700 mm). With a total of 1670 sunshine hours per year, Regensburg is roughly 120 hours above German average.[2]<br/><br/>The warmest month of the year, on average, is July. The coolest month of the year, on average, is January.<br/>:[3] in the Neuhaussaal.[4] Both figures show, that Regensburg is behind other Bavarian cities in this context. Therefore, the municipal government presented an energy plan in 2014, which should enhance the transformation towards renewable energy sources over the next decade.<br/><br/>Regensburg hosts one of the most modern university hospitals in Europe, the Universitätsklinikum Regensburg. Aside, there are several other renowned hospitals such as the Krankenhaus Barmherzige Brüder and the St. Josef-Krankenhaus. In the Bezirksklinikum, mental diseases are treated. With 19,4 hospital beds per 1000 residents, Regensburg owns the fourth highest density of beds per residents in Germany.[5] Concerning medical doctors per residents, Regensburg obtains the third place in Germany (339 per 100,000 residents).[6]<br/><br/>The city's BioPark, representing Bavaria's second largest biotech cluster, hosts numerous research institutions and biotech companies.Since 1874 there has been a College of Catholic Music, the Hochschule für Katholische Kirchenmusik und Musikpädagogik Regensburg..[7](The city has a population of 150,894 <small>(December 31, 2017)</small> and is thus fourth after Munich, Nuremberg and Augsburg among the large cities of the Free State of Bavaria.<br/>It is the episcopal see of the diocese Regensburg, has three universities and is one of the 3 regional centers in Bavaria.<br/><ref>[ Ordinance amending the regulation on the state development program Bavaria], Ed.: Bavarian State Ministry of Finance, for State Development and Homeland, 2018-02-21.</ref><br /><br/>{{#display_map:<br/>&#124;centre=regensburg<br/>&#124;service=leaflet<br/>}}<br/><br />defzoom=10<br/>}}<br/>==Geography==<br/>===Topography===<br/>Regensburg is situated on the northernmost part of the Danube river at the geological crossroads of four distinct landscapes:<br/>*to the north and northeast lies the Bavarian Forest (Bayerischer Wald) with granite and gneiss mountains, wide forests and its national park<br/>*to the east and south-east is the fertile Danube plain (Gäuboden) which are highly cultivated loess plains<br/>*the south is dominated by the tertiary hill country (Tertiär-Hügelland), a continuation of Alpine foothills<br/>*to the West is Franconian Jura (Fränkische Jura)<br/>===Climate===<br/>The climate in Regensburg is categorized in the Köppen climate classification as Dfb (humid continental). The average temperature of 8.5&nbsp;°C is slightly above the German average (7.8&nbsp;°C), the average precipitation of 636&nbsp;mm per year below the German average (approximately 700&nbsp;mm). With a total of 1670 sunshine hours per year, Regensburg is roughly 120 hours above German average.<ref name="uni-regensburg"><br/>The warmest month of the year, on average, is July. The coolest month of the year, on average, is January.<br/>==Gallery==<br/><gallery><br/>File:Stadtansicht Regensburg.JPG&#124;Bridge tower and Salt shed<br/>File:Regensburg Steinerne thionchar na n-aibhneacha Danbue, Naab agus Regen.Le níos mó ná 140,000 cónaitheoirí, is é Regenburg an ceathrú cathair is mó i Stát Bavaria (ó Laidin Castra Regina, go déanach freisin. Ratisbona agus RatisponaTá daonra de 150,894 (Nollaig 31, 2017) agus is é an ceathrú ceann tar éis München, Nuremberg agus Augustburg é. Is í an chathair lár polaitiúil, eacnamaíoch agus cultúrtha Oirthear na Baváire agus príomhchathair an réigiúin riaracháin Bavarian Uachtarach Phlatate. Suíomh Oidhreachta Domhanda de chuid UNESCO é lár na cathrach agus fianaise ar stádas na cathrach mar lárionad cultúrtha na Gearmáine sa Mheán-Aois. Sa bhliain 2014, bhí Regenburg i measc na bpríomh-speántas agus na n-áiteanna taistil sa Ghearmáin.[1] Ar a dtugtar Ratisbon go ginearálta sa fichiú haois, tugtar Ratsbonne ar an gcathair mar Ratisbone sa Fhraincis agus mar Ratisbona san Iodáilis, sa Phortaingéilis agus sa Spáinnis. i measc na cathracha móra an Saorstát na Baváire saor in aisce.<br/><br/>Is é an t-eipsealapal a fheiceáil ar an dísle Regenburg, tá trí ollscoil aige agus tá sé ar cheann de na 3 ionad réigiúnacha sa Bavaria. [1]<br/><br/>Déantar an aeráid i Regenburg a chatagóiriú in aicmiú aeráide Köppen mar Dfb (mór-roinn). Is é an meánteocht de 8.5 °C beagán os cionn mheán na Gearmáine (7.8 °C), an meán-fhrasaíocht 636 mm in aghaidh na bliana faoi bhun mheán na Gearmáine (thart ar 700 mm). Le 1670 uair an chloig solas na gréine in aghaidh na bliana, tá Regenburg thart ar 120 uair an chloig os cionn meán na Gearmáine.[2]<br/><br/>Is é mí Iúil an mhí is teo den bhliain, ar an meán.Is í mí Iúil an mhí is fuaire den bhliain, ar an meán Eanáir.<br/>: [3] sa Neusal.[4] Taispeánann an dá fhigiúr, go bhfuil Regenburg taobh thiar de chathracha Bavarian eile sa chomhthéacs seo. Dá bhrí sin, chuir an rialtas bardasach plean fuinnimh i láthair in 2014, plean ar cheart dó feabhas a chur ar an athrú i dtreo foinsí fuinnimh in-athnuaite sna deich mbliana atá romhainn.<br/><br/>Tá ceann de na hospidéil ollscoile is nua-aimseartha san Eoraip, na hÚraitheoiríätskilinkum Regenburg.side, tá roinnt ospidéal clúiteach eile ann mar an mBanrchkenhaus Barmherzige Braüder agus an St Josef-Krankenhaus. Sa Bezirkskilnikum, déantar galair mheabhrach a chóireáil. Le 19,4 leaba ospidéil in aghaidh an 1000 cónaitheoir, tá an ceathrú dlús is airde de leapacha in aghaidh na Gearmáine ag Regenburg.[5] Maidir le dochtúirí leighis in aghaidh na n-áitritheoirí, faigheann Regenburg an tríú áit sa Ghearmáin (339 in aghaidh na 100,000 cónaitheoirí).[6]<br/><br/>Is iomaí institiúid taighde agus comhlacht bithteicneolaíochta atá in BithPark na cathrach, a dhéanann ionadaíocht ar an dara braisle ba mhó sa bhithéiteach i mBavaria. Ó 1874 tá Coláiste Ceoil Caitliceach, an Hochschule für Katolsche Kirkmusik und Musikpädagogik Regenburg. [7] (Tá daonra de 150,894 <all>(Nollaig 31, 2017), </ beag> agus mar sin tá sé i measc na gcathracha móra de chuid Saorstát na Baváire.<br/>Is é an t-eipsealapal a fheiceáil ar an dísle Regenburg, tá trí ollscoil ann agus tá sé ar cheann de na 3 ionad réigiúnacha sa Bavaria.<br/><ref> [Ordance ag leasú an rialacháin maidir le clár forbartha an stáit Baváire], Ed: Bavarian State Minister of Finance, um Fhorbairt Stáit agus um Ísiltír, 2018-02-21.</ref> <b/><br/>{_Mapa:<br/>&#124; ionad = regenburg<br/>&#124;seirbhís = bileog<br/>}}<br/><b />defzoom = 10<br/>}}<br/>== Tíreolaíocht ==<br/>== Topagrafaíocht ==<br/>Tá Regenburg suite ar an gcuid is faide ó thuaidh d’abhainn Dhúibe ag crosbhóthar geolaíochta ceithre thírdhreach ar leith:<br/>* Tá an Foraoise Bavarian (Byeriscer Wald) le sléibhte eibhir agus géine, foraoisí leathan agus a pháirc náisiúnta<br/>*go dtí an taobh thoir agus ó dheas tá an plean Danóibe torthúil (Gäuboden) a bhfuil machairí chailleann an- saothraithe acu<br/>*tá an taobh ó dheas den tír is mó atá ar an mbealach treasach (Tertiär-Hügelland), a leanann de chosáin Alpach<br/>* Is é an t-Iarthar Juan Francian (Fränkische Jura)<br/>== Aeráid ===<br/>Déantar an aeráid i Regenburg a chatagóiriú in aicmiú aeráide Köppen mar Dfb (mór-roinn). Is é an meánteocht de 8.5&nsp; °C beagán os cionn mheán na Gearmáine (7.8&nbsp; °C), an meán-fhrascaireacht de 636&nbsp; mm in aghaidh na bliana faoi bhun mheán na Gearmáine (thart ar 700 & nbsp;mm). Le 1670 uair an chloig solas na gréine in aghaidh na bliana, tá Regenburg thart ar 120 uair an chloig os cionn meán na Gearmáine.<br/>Is é mí Iúil an mhí is teo den bhliain, ar an meán.Is í mí Iúil an mhí is fuaire den bhliain, ar an meán Eanáir.<br/>== Gailearaí ==<br/><galery><br/>Comhad:Standsicht Regenburg.JPG &#124;Túr Droichead agus Seilfeanna<br/>Comhad:Ghníomhaireacht Steinerne Bruce.jpg ==<br/>=== amharclanna ==: Ainm <ref==== ainm an bhéargú ar an drochuair == Imeachtaí ======= Oíche an tsruthúlacht =====<br/>Le níos mó ná 500 barraí, bialanna, clubanna agus áiteanna eile amháin sa chathair inmheánach amháin, soláthraíonn Regenburg saol oíche saibhir agus éagsúil mar gheall ar a dhaonra óg.<br/>= = Déimeagrafaic ===<br/>== Daonra ==== Polaitíochta ==<br/>== Rialtas ===== Bóiroughs ===== Bonneagar ==<br/>== Iompar === Is é líonra bus á rith ag an [VVV (Regenburger Verkehrsverband) an t-iompar áitiúil.<br/>== Fuinneamh====== Sláinte == Páirc an Bhitháirigh is mó, a dhéanann óstáil ar an dara braisle de bhithteicneolaíochta is mó sa chathair, a bhfuil go leor institiúidí taighde agus comhlachtaí bithteicneolaíochta ann.<br/>= Oideachas ===<br/>== Ollscoileanna agus lucht acadúil == Ó 1874 tá Coláiste Ceoil Chaitliceacha, an Für Katholichemusic, und Musikpädigoki Regenburg.<br/>== Taighde ==== Scoileanna ==== Teangacha ghaolmhara ====<br/>{MediaWiki: t-eipsealapal a fheiceáil ar an dísle Regenburg, tá trí ollscoil ann agus tá sé ar cheann de na 3 ionad réigiúnacha sa Bavaria.<br/><br/>+<br/><br/><ref> [Ordance ag leasú an rialacháin maidir le clár institiúid taighde agus comhlacht bithteicneolaíochta atá in BithPark na cathrach, a dhéanann ionadaíocht ar an dara braisle ba mhó sa bhithéiteach i mBavaria.<br/><br/>−<br/><br/>−<br/><br/>=
